# Fault Localization: iwlwifi Missing PCI Subdevice Entries

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of torvalds/linux)
- **Kernel Version**: 5.6-rc2
- **Difficulty**: expert
- **Category**: fault_localization
- **Subsystem**: Drivers
- **Component**: network-wireless (Intel iwlwifi)

## Bug Report

**Bug ID**: 206661
**Summary**: iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526 (0x04010, 0x4018 and 0x401C)
**Regression**: Yes

I am using Kernel 5.6 RC2 and I am seeing issues where firmware is not being loaded for my Intel Corporation Wireless-AC 9260 card. Attached is the boot logging.

If I can do anything to debug, let me know.

## Task

You are a fault localization agent. Given the bug report above, your task is to identify the **exact source file(s)** and **function(s)/data structure(s)** in the Linux kernel source tree (at `/workspace`) that need to be modified to fix this bug.

You must:
1. Analyze the bug report to understand the symptoms and context
2. Search the kernel source code to identify the relevant subsystem and files
3. Narrow down to the specific file(s) and function(s)/data structure(s) that contain the bug or need modification
4. Write your findings to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` in the following format:

```json
{
  "buggy_files": ["path/to/file.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["function_or_struct_name"],
  "confidence": 0.8,
  "reasoning": "Brief explanation of why these locations are the fault"
}
```

**Important**: Paths should be relative to the kernel source root (e.g., `kernel/sched/core.c`, not `/workspace/kernel/sched/core.c`).

## Success Criteria

- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy file(s)
- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy function(s) or data structure(s)
- [ ] Write results to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json`
- [ ] Provide reasoning for the localization

82-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have successfully completed the fault localization task. Let me summarize my findings:

## Fault Localization Summary

**Bug**: iwlwifi missing PCI subdevice entries for Intel 9260 wireless card (device 0x2526) preventing firmware loading.

**Root Cause**: The `iwl_dev_info_table` in `drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c` is missing device info entries for subdevice IDs 0x4010, 0x4018, and 0x401C.

**Key Evidence**:
1. The file contains a static device info table that maps PCI device/subdevice ID pairs to firmware configurations
2. For Intel 9260 (0x2526), the table includes entries for multiple firmware variant codes:
   - 0x00xx prefix: 0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C
   - 0x60xx prefix: 0x6010, 0x6014
   - 0x80xx prefix: 0x8010, 0x8014
   - 0xA0xx prefix: 0xA014
   - 0xE0xx prefix: 0xE010, 0xE014
   - But **0x40xx entries are missing**: 0x4010, 0x4018, 0x401C

3. Without these entries in the device info table, the driver cannot properly match the device and load the correct firmware configuration, causing the reported firmware loading failure.

**Result**: Created `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` with the identified buggy file and data structure.

{
  "buggy_files": [
    "drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c"
  ],
  "buggy_functions": [
    "iwl_dev_info_table"
  ],
  "confidence": 0.85,
  "reasoning": "The bug report indicates missing PCI subdevice entries for Intel 9260 card (device ID 0x2526) with subdevice IDs 0x4010, 0x4018, and 0x401C. Analysis of the iwlwifi driver code shows that the file drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c contains two PCI device ID tables: (1) the iwl_hw_card_ids PCI device table (lines 84-868) which provides fallback matching with PCI_ANY_ID, and (2) the iwl_dev_info_table (lines 978-997) which provides more specific firmware configuration mapping for exact device ID matches. The dev_info_table is crucial for proper firmware loading as it maps device IDs to specific firmware configurations. The 9260 variant entries follow a clear pattern in the dev_info_table with different firmware revision code prefixes (0x00xx, 0x60xx, 0x80xx, 0xA0xx, 0xE0xx), but are missing entries for the 0x40xx prefix (specifically 0x4010, 0x4018, 0x401C) which correspond to additional 9260 board variants. Without these entries, the driver cannot properly identify and load the correct firmware for these device variants, causing the firmware loading failure reported in the bug."
}
